ACTOR FMiniAlien 7468
{
	DropItem "HealthHeart" 210
	DropItem "PowerslaveSpawner" 64
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 8
	Health 550
	Radius 16
	Height 30
	Mass 400 
	Speed 16
	MeleeDamage 8
	Scale 0.64
	Damage 3
	PainChance 30
	Minmissilechance 64
	Monster	+DONTCORPSE RipLevelMin 1 
	BloodColor GreenYellow
	+BOSS
	+AMBUSH
	+FLOORCLIP 
	SeeSound "q2mutant/sight" 
	AttackSound "q2mutant/meleeswing"
	PainSound "q2mutant/pain" 
	DeathSound "q2mutant/death" 
	ActiveSound "q2mutant/seeking" 
	MeleeSound "q2mutant/meleehit"
	Obituary "%o now believes in the monsters from movies."
	PainChance "Charm", 255
	PainChance "Terror", 255
	PainChance "Defile", 255
	PainChance "Drain", 153
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 255
//Armor							 //they're supossed to have a hard skin
	DamageFactor "Electric", 1.5
	DamageFactor "Plasma", 0.75
	DamageFactor "PlasmaDisint", 0.75
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.5
	States
	{
	Pain.Charm:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)
		Goto See
	Pain.Terror:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)
		Goto See
	Pain.Drain:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto Pain
	Pain.Defile:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("DefileCheck",1)
		Goto See
	
	Spawn:
		ALIE A 4 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		ALIE AABBCCDD 3 A_Chase
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,2)
		TNT1 A 0
		Loop
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(15,"Death")
		Loop
	Melee:
		ALIE E 6 A_FaceTarget
		ALIE F 6 A_FaceTarget
		ALIE G 6 A_MeleeAttack
		Goto See
	Missile:
		ALIE E 1 A_FaceTarget
		ALIE F 6 A_SkullAttack
		Loop
	Pain:
		ALIE H 5
		ALIE H 5 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:	
		"####" "#" 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"Defilement")
		ALIE I 6
		ALIE J 6 A_Scream
		ALIE K 6 A_NoBlocking
		ALIE L 6
		ALIE M 6
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		ALIE NNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNN 5 A_Explode(5,16)
		ALIE N -1
		Stop
	Defilement:
	DefileDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RedMiteSpawner",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto XDeathBlood
	XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"DefileDeath")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,"XDeathBlood")
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GreenGib",0,0,random(1,5),0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 AAAA 0 A_TossGib
		Goto Death
	XDeathBlood:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GreenGibSp",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 AAAAAA 0 A_TossGib
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		Stop
	Raise:
		ALIE NMLKJI 4
		Goto See
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_SetTranslation(0,50)	
		ALIE H 1 A_FadeOut(0.015)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		TNT1 a 0 A_Stop	
		TNT1 a 0 A_Fall
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateShadowMedium",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateSparksMedium",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		ALIE HH 2 A_FadeOut(0.03)
		Goto Disintegrate+6
	}
}

ACTOR FAlien 7469	// hell knight

	+FLOORCLIP

	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 255

	{

		Goto See
	Pain.Terror:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)
		Goto See
	Pain.Drain:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto Pain
	Pain.Defile:
		TNT1 A 0

		Goto See
	
	Spawn:
		ALIE A 4 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		ALIE AABBCCDD 3 A_Chase
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,2)
		TNT1 A 0
		Loop
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(5,"Death")
		Loop
	Melee:
		ALIE E 6 A_FaceTarget
		ALIE F 6 A_FaceTarget
		ALIE G 6 A_MeleeAttack
		Goto See
	Missile:
		ALIE E 1 A_FaceTarget
		ALIE F 6 A_SkullAttack
		Loop
	Pain:
		ALIE H 5
		ALIE H 5 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:	
		"####" "#" 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"Defilement")
		ALIE I 6
		ALIE J 6 A_Scream
		ALIE K 6 A_NoBlocking
		ALIE L 6
		ALIE M 6
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		ALIE NNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNNN 5 A_Explode(5,16)
		ALIE N -1
		Stop
		TNT1 A 0 A_Die
		TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RedMiteSpawner",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto XDeathBlood
	XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"Defilement")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,"XDeathBlood")
		TNT1 AAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GreenGib",0,0,random(1,5),0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 AAAAAAA 0 A_TossGib
		Goto Death
	XDeathBlood:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
		TNT1 AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GreenGibSp",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 AAAAAAAA 0 A_TossGib
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		Stop
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_SetTranslation(0,50)	
		ALIE H 1 A_FadeOut(0.015)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		TNT1 a 0 A_Stop

		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateShadowMedium",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateSparksMedium",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)

		Goto Disintegrate+6
	Raise:
		ALIE NMLKJI 4
		Goto See
	}

ACTOR Predator 7504	// arachnotron
{
	DropItem "CellAmmo"
	DropItem "HealthHeart" 210
	DropItem "PowerslaveSpawner" 28
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 8
	Health 700
	Radius 20
	Height 64
	Speed 12
	PainChance 160
	Mass 800
	Monster	+DONTCORPSE RipLevelMin 1 
	RenderStyle Fuzzy
	BloodColor Green
//	+Stealth
	+BOSSDEATH
	+FLOORCLIP
	+DONTSPLASH
	+DONTMORPH
	REACTIONTIME 32
	Scale 0.9
	Obituary "%o fell prey to the predator."
	DeathSound "q2bosstank/pain3"
	PainSound "q2bosstank/pain2"
	SeeSound "q2bosstank/sight"
	ActiveSound "q2bosstank/search"
	PainChance "Charm", 96
	PainChance "Terror", 96
	PainChance "Drain", 64
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 128
	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 128
//Flesh
	DamageFactor "Electric", 1.5
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 1.5
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 2.0
	States
	{
	Pain.Charm:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)
		Goto See
	Pain.Terror:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)
		Goto See
	Pain.Drain:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto Pain
	Spawn:
		PRED A 4 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		PRED A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		PRED AABBCCDD 3 A_Chase
		Goto See+1
	Missile:
		PRED G 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,0)
		PRED EEEEEEEEEE 1 A_FadeIn
		PRED A 0 A_Jump(32,37)
		PRED E 6 A_FaceTarget
		PRED E 1 A_FaceTarget
		PRED F 2 Bright A_CustomMissile("PredatorBeam3",40,5,0)
		PRED E 1 A_FaceTarget
		PRED F 2 Bright A_CustomMissile("PredatorBeam3",40,5,0)
		PRED E 1 A_FaceTarget
		PRED F 2 Bright A_CustomMissile("PredatorBeam3",40,5,0)
		PRED E 1 A_FaceTarget
		PRED F 2 Bright A_CustomMissile("PredatorBeam3",40,5,0)
		PRED E 1 A_FaceTarget
		PRED F 2 Bright A_CustomMissile("PredatorBeam3",40,5,0)
		PRED E 1 A_FaceTarget
		PRED F 2 Bright A_CustomMissile("PredatorBeam3",40,5,0)
		PRED E 1 A_FaceTarget
		PRED F 2 Bright A_CustomMissile("PredatorBeam3",40,5,0)
		PRED E 1 A_FaceTarget
		PRED F 2 Bright A_CustomMissile("PredatorBeam3",40,5,0)
		PRED E 1 A_FaceTarget
		PRED F 2 Bright A_CustomMissile("PredatorBeam3",40,5,0)
		PRED E 1 A_FaceTarget
		PRED F 2 Bright A_CustomMissile("PredatorBeam3",40,5,0)
		PRED E 1 A_FaceTarget
		PRED F 2 Bright A_CustomMissile("PredatorBeam3",40,5,0)
		PRED E 1 A_FaceTarget
		PRED F 2 Bright A_CustomMissile("PredatorBeam3",40,5,0)
		PRED E 1 A_FaceTarget
		PRED EEEEEEEEE 1 A_FadeOut
		PRED E 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,2)
	  Goto See
		PRED EEEEE 4 A_FaceTarget
		PRED F 8 Bright A_CustomMissile("PredatorBeam",40,5,0)
		PRED E 8 A_FaceTarget
		PRED EEEEEEEEE 1 A_FadeOut
		PRED E 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,2)
	  Goto See
	Pain:
		PRED G 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		PRED G 3 A_SetTranslucent(1,0)
	  PRED G 3 A_Pain
		PRED GGGGGGGGG 1 A_FadeOut
		PRED G 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,2)
		PRED G 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
	  Goto See
	Death:
			
		"####" "#" 0 A_UnsetSolid
		PRED H 4 A_Scream
		PRED I 4 A_Fall
		PRED JK 4
		PRED L 6
		PRED MNO 4
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		PRED P -1 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,"None","AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GreenGibSp",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 AAAAAA 0 A_TossGib
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,"None","AEoDSpawner")
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		Stop
	Ice:
		PRED G 5 A_GenericFreezeDeath
		PRED G 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,"None","AEoDSpawner")
		PRED G 1 A_FreezeDeathChunks
		Wait
	Raise:
		PRED PONMLKJIH 4
		Goto See
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1.0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_SetTranslation(0,50)	
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,"None","AEoDSpawner")
		PRED G 1 A_FadeOut(0.015)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		TNT1 a 0 A_Stop	
		TNT1 a 0 A_Fall
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateShadowMedium",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateSparksMedium",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		PRED GG 2 A_FadeOut(0.03)
		Goto Disintegrate+8
	}
}


actor PredatorBeam
{
	Radius 6
	Height 8
	Speed 35
	Damage 15
	Scale 0.6
	PROJECTILE
	SeeSound "imp/attack"
	DeathSound "imp/shotx"
	Translation "192:207=218:223"
	DamageType "Plasma"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		ZAP5 ABCD 3 Bright
		Loop
	Death:
		ZAP5 A 1 Bright A_FadeOut
		Wait
	}
}

Actor PredatorBlader
{
	+EXTREMEDEATH
	Projectile
	Damage 20
	Speed 20
	Radius 10
	Height 10
	Scale 0.4
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		TNT1 A 0
	R001 K 0 A_PlaySound("reilsss/weapons/painkillerspin", 6, 1.0, 1)	
	R001 KLMN 1
		Loop
	Death:
	Crash:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound ("reilsss/weapons/katanametal")
		TNT1 A 2
		Stop
	XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("reilsss/weapons/katanahit")
		Stop
	}
}

		Stop
	}

ACTOR SnakeOTaur 7507	// hell knight
{
	DropItem "Mana2Ammo"
	DropItem "HealthHeart" 210
	DropItem "PowerslaveSpawner" 28
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 8
	Health  700
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Scale 0.65
	Mass 2003	//I wonder why it have such specific mass amount... 
	Speed 12
	PainChance 10
	MeleeDamage 16
	Monster	+DONTCORPSE RipLevelMin 1
	+FLOORCLIP
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+LONGMELEERANGE
	+SHORTMISSILERANGE
	SeeSound "SANDERSON/SITE"
	PainSound "SANDERSON/PAIN"
	DeathSound "SANDERSON/DEATH"
	ActiveSound "SANDERSON/ACTIVE"
	MeleeSound "SANDERSON/SWOOSH"
	HitObituary "the SNAKE O TAUR beat the crap out of POOR %o."
	PainChance "Charm", 192
	PainChance "Terror", 192
	PainChance "Defile", 255
	PainChance "Drain", 110
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 255
//Flesh
	DamageFactor "Electric", 1.5
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 1.5
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 2.0
	States
	{
	Pain.Charm:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)
		Goto See
	Pain.Terror:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)
		Goto See
	Pain.Drain:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto Pain
	Pain.Defile:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("DefileCheck",1)
		Goto See
	Spawn:
		DUKE D 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		DUKE AABBCCDD 3 A_Chase
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,2)
		TNT1 A 0
		Loop
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(5,"Death")
		Loop
	Melee:
		DUKE DE 6 A_FaceTarget
		DUKE F 8 A_MeleeAttack
		Goto See
	Pain:
		DUKE G 4
		DUKE G 4 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Burn:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"Defilement")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Fall
		TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
		DUKE WXYZ 5 A_FadeOut
		DUKE [ 1 A_FadeOut
		Wait
	Death:	
		"####" "#" 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"Defilement")
		DUKE L 8
		DUKE M 8 A_Scream
		DUKE N 6
		DUKE O 6 A_Fall
		DUKE PQRSTU 6 A_TossGib
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		DUKE V  -1
		Stop
	Defilement:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Die
		TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RedMiteSpawner",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto XDeathBlood
	XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"Defilement")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,"XDeathBlood")
		TNT1 AAAAAAAAAA 0 A_TossGib
		Goto Death
	XDeathBlood:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
		TNT1 AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BloodGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		Stop
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_SetTranslation(0,50)	
	DUKE G 1 A_FadeOut(0.015)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		TNT1 a 0 A_Stop	
		TNT1 a 0 A_Fall
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateShadowMedium",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateSparksMedium",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
	DUKE GG 2 A_FadeOut(0.03)
		Goto Disintegrate+6
	Raise:
		DUKE VT 8
		DUKE QP 6
		Goto See
	}
}

// Lasercannon puff
Actor Laserpuff2
{
	Mass 1
	Radius 1
	Height 1
	+NOBLOCKMAP
	+NOGRAVITY
	+PUFFONACTORS
	RenderStyle Add
	alpha 0.5
	DamageType "Plasma"
	states
	{
	spawn:
		LPUF ABCDE 4 BRIGHT
		stop
	}
}

ACTOR NaziGuard 7509	// nazi
{
	DropItem "BulletAmmo" 32
	DropItem "ShellAmmo" 32
	DropItem "CellAmmo" 32
	DropItem "ExploAmmo" 32
	DropItem "HealthHeart" 210
	DropItem "PowerslaveSpawner" 128
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 8
	Health 30
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Damage 1
	Speed 9
	Painchance 200
	SeeSound "Guardsight"
	PainSound "Guardpain"
	AttackSound "Pistol"
	DeathSound "Guarddeath"
	ActiveSound "Guardact"
	Monster	+DONTCORPSE RipLevelMin 1
	+FLOORCLIP
	Obituary "%o was shot by a Nazi Guard."
	PainChance "Charm", 255
	PainChance "Terror", 255
	PainChance "Defile", 255
	PainChance "Drain", 160
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 255
//Armor
	DamageFactor "Electric", 1.5
	DamageFactor "Plasma", 0.75
	DamageFactor "PlasmaDisint", 0.75
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.5
	States
	{
	Pain.Charm:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)
		Goto See
	Pain.Terror:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)
		Goto See
	Pain.Drain:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto Pain
	Pain.Defile:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("DefileCheck",1)
		Goto See
	Spawn:
		GURD AB 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		GURD AABBCCDD 4 A_Chase
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,2)
		TNT1 A 0
		Loop
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(15,"Death")
		Loop
	Missile:
		GURD E 3 A_FaceTarget(0,0)
		"----" A 0 A_CustomMissile("BulletTracerFX",20,0,random(-(1),1),CMF_OFFSETPITCH,random(-(1),1))
		GURD F 5 BRIGHT A_CustomBulletAttack (1,1,1,3,"BulletDamagePuff")
		Goto See
	Pain:
		GURD G 1 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:	
		"####" "#" 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"Defilement")
		GURD H 5 A_Scream
		GURD I 5 A_Fall
		GURD JK 5
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		GURD L -1
		Stop
	Defilement:
		TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RedMiteSpawner",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto XDeathBlood
	XDeath:	
		"####" "#" 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"Defilement")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,"XDeathBlood")
		TNT1 AAAAAA 0 A_TossGib
		GURD M 5
		GURD N 5 A_XScream
		GURD O 5 A_Fall
		GURD PQRST 5
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		GURD U -1
		Stop
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RedMiteSpawner",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto XDeathBlood
	XDeathBlood:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BloodGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		Stop
	Raise:
		GURD KJIH 4
		Goto See
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_SetTranslation(0,50)	
		GURD G 1 A_FadeOut(0.015)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		TNT1 a 0 A_Stop	
		TNT1 a 0 A_Fall
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateShadowMedium",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateSparksMedium",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		GURD GG 2 A_FadeOut(0.03)
		Goto Disintegrate+6
	}
}

ACTOR NaziCommander 7510	// nazi
{
	DropItem "BulletAmmo" 32
	DropItem "ShellAmmo" 32
	DropItem "CellAmmo" 32
	DropItem "ExploAmmo" 32
	DropItem "HealthHeart" 210
	DropItem "PowerslaveSpawner" 128
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 8
	Health 45
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Damage 1
	Speed 8
	Painchance 150
	SeeSound "Guardsight"
	AttackSound "Rifle1"
	PainSound "Guardpain"
	DeathSound "Guarddeath"
	ActiveSound "Guardact"
	Monster	+DONTCORPSE RipLevelMin 1
	+FLOORCLIP
	Obituary "%o was terminated by a Nazi Commander."
	PainChance "Charm", 255
	PainChance "Terror", 255
	PainChance "Defile", 255
	PainChance "Drain", 160
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 255
//Armor
	DamageFactor "Electric", 1.5
	DamageFactor "Plasma", 0.75
	DamageFactor "PlasmaDisint", 0.75
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.5
	States
	{
	Pain.Charm:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)
		Goto See
	Pain.Terror:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)
		Goto See
	Pain.Drain:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto Pain
	Pain.Defile:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("DefileCheck",1)
		Goto See
	Spawn:
		OFCR AB 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		OFCR AABBCCDD 4 A_Chase
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,2)
		TNT1 A 0
		Loop
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(15,"Death")
		Loop
	Missile:
		OFCR E 1 A_FaceTarget(0,0)
		"----" A 0 A_CustomMissile("BulletTracerFX",20,0,random(-(3),3),CMF_OFFSETPITCH,random(-(3),3))
		OFCR F 3 BRIGHT A_CustomBulletAttack (3,3,1,2,"BulletDamagePuff")
		OFCR E 1 A_FaceTarget
		OFCR E 1 A_CposRefire
		Loop
	Pain:
		OFCR G 1 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:	
		"####" "#" 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"Defilement")
		OFCR H 5 A_Scream
		OFCR I 5 A_Fall
		OFCR JKLM 5
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		OFCR N -1
		Stop
	Defilement:
		TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RedMiteSpawner",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto XDeathBlood
	XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"Defilement")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,"XDeathBlood")
		TNT1 AAAAAA 0 A_TossGib
		OFCR O 5
		OFCR P 5 A_XScream
		OFCR Q 5 A_Fall
		OFCR RS 5
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		OFCR T -1
		Stop
	XDeathBlood:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BloodGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		Stop
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_SetTranslation(0,50)	
		OFCR G 1 A_FadeOut(0.015)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		TNT1 a 0 A_Stop	
		TNT1 a 0 A_Fall
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateShadowMedium",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateSparksMedium",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		OFCR GG 2 A_FadeOut(0.03)
		Goto Disintegrate+6
	Raise:
		OFCR NMLKJIH 4
		Goto See
	}
}

Actor NMRocket
{
	Projectile
	Radius 6
	Height 6
	Speed 24
	Damage 5
	Scale 0.3
	SeeSound "weapons/rocketlaunch"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
	SWMS A 2
		Loop
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(32,32)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("NewExplosionSmall",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		Stop
	}
}

ACTOR NaziGuard2 7513		// nazi
{
	DropItem "BulletAmmo" 32
	DropItem "ShellAmmo" 32
	DropItem "CellAmmo" 32
	DropItem "ExploAmmo" 32
	DropItem "HealthHeart" 210
	DropItem "PowerslaveSpawner" 128
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 8
	Health 45
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Speed 12
	Painchance 200
	SeeSound "Guardsight"
	PainSound "Guardpain"
	AttackSound "Pistol2"
	DeathSound "Guarddeath"
	ActiveSound "Guardact"
	Monster	+DONTCORPSE RipLevelMin 1
	+FLOORCLIP
	Obituary "%o was hit by a Nazi Guard."
	PainChance "Charm", 255
	PainChance "Terror", 255
	PainChance "Defile", 255
	PainChance "Drain", 160
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 255
//Armor
	DamageFactor "Electric", 1.5
	DamageFactor "Plasma", 0.75
	DamageFactor "PlasmaDisint", 0.75
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.5
	States
	{
	Pain.Charm:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)
		Goto See
	Pain.Terror:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)
		Goto See
	Pain.Drain:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto Pain
	Pain.Defile:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("DefileCheck",1)
		Goto See
	Spawn:
		GUR2 AB 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		GUR2 AABBCCDD 4 A_Chase
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,2)
		TNT1 A 0
		Loop
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(15,"Death")
		Loop
	Missile:
		GUR2 E 3 A_FaceTarget(0,0)
		"----" AA 0 A_CustomMissile("BulletTracerFX",20,0,random(-(4),4),CMF_OFFSETPITCH,random(-(3),3))
		GUR2 F 5 BRIGHT A_CustomBulletAttack (4,3,2,4,"BulletDamagePuff")
		GUR2 E 3 A_FaceTarget(0,0)
		"----" AA 0 A_CustomMissile("BulletTracerFX",20,0,random(-(3),3),CMF_OFFSETPITCH,random(-(3),3))
		GUR2 F 5 BRIGHT A_CustomBulletAttack (3,3,2,4,"BulletDamagePuff")
		GUR2 E 3 A_FaceTarget(0,0)
		"----" AA 0 A_CustomMissile("BulletTracerFX",20,0,random(-(4),4),CMF_OFFSETPITCH,random(-(4),4))
		GUR2 F 5 BRIGHT A_CustomBulletAttack (4,4,2,4,"BulletDamagePuff")
		Goto See
	Pain:
		GUR2 G 4 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:	
		"####" "#" 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"Defilement")
		GUR2 H 5 A_Scream
		GUR2 I 5 A_Fall
		GUR2 JK 5
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		GUR2 L -1
		Stop
		Defilement:
		TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RedMiteSpawner",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto XDeathBlood
	XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"Defilement")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,"XDeathBlood")
		TNT1 AAAAAA 0 A_TossGib
		GUR2 M 5
		GUR2 N 5 A_XScream
		GUR2 O 5 A_Fall
		GUR2 PQRST 5
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		GUR2 U -1
		Stop
	XDeathBlood:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BloodGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		Stop
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_SetTranslation(0,50)	
		GUR2 G 1 A_FadeOut(0.015)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		TNT1 a 0 A_Stop	
		TNT1 a 0 A_Fall
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateShadowMedium",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateSparksMedium",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		GUR2 GG 2 A_FadeOut(0.03)
		Goto Disintegrate+6
	Raise:
		GUR2 LKJIH 4
		Goto See
	}
}

//=====================================================================================

//=====================================================================================
//=====================================================================================

//   No type
//The Hard-to-kill OmoiCaco.
//This creature was inspired by the Omoikane enemy of Shin Megami Tensei: Digital Devil Saga 1 and 2.
//Basically the OmoiCaco attacks until it ends up in it's pain state.  If it does, then it will tell
//you that you get no reward today, then simply disappear from the level all together.  For this matter,
//the OmoiCaco does NOT count towards 100% kills.
Actor OmoiCaco : FCacodemon
{
	obituary "%o was fried by the incredibly rare OmoiCaco!"
	hitobituary "%o managed to somehow get eaten by the OmoiCaco."
	speed 2
	scale 0.3
	radius 10
	height 23
	health 60
	painchance 128
	bloodcolor green
	seesound "monster/omoicaco/see"
	deathsound "monster/omoicaco/death"
	Translation "168:191=192:207","192:207=112:127","112:127=80:111","16:47=193:207","224:231=168:175"
	+NODAMAGE
	+FLOORCLIP
	-COUNTKILL
	+DONTMORPH
	+NOFEAR
	+NOTIMEFREEZE
	DamageFactor "ChaosExpl1", 0
	DamageFactor "ChaosExpl2", 0
	states
	{
	Spawn:
		HEAD A 1 A_Look
		loop
	See:
		HEAD A 1 A_ExtChase(0,96)
		loop
	Missile:
		HEAD BBBBCCC 1 A_FaceTarget
		HEAD D 0 A_Jump(160,6)
		HEAD C 1 A_ChangeFlag(NODAMAGE,0)
		HEAD D 2 A_CustomMissile("CacodemonBall",10,0,0)
		HEAD D 0 A_FaceTarget
		HEAD D 1 A_ChangeFlag(NODAMAGE,1)
		HEAD D 1 A_FaceTarget
		goto See
		HEAD D 4 A_CustomMissile("CacodemonBall",10,0,0)
		goto See
	Pain:
		HEAD B 0 A_SetInvulnerable
		HEAD B 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		HEAD B 3 A_Print("You get no reward today!  HAHAHAHAHAHAHAHAHAAAAAAA!!!!")
		HEAD CBABCBABCBABCBA 3
		HEAD B 0 A_SpawnItem("TeleportFog",0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 // A_Die
		stop
	Death:
		HEAD B 0 A_JumpIf(health < -60,"Ded2much")
		HEAD B 3 A_Print("Damn it!  You got me!!!")
		HEAD CBABCBABCBABCBA 3
		HEAD G 4 A_Scream
		HEAD HIJK 4
		HEAD A 0 A_Jump(180,2)
		HEAD A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Yashichi",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto WeaponDrop
		HEAD AAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Q2BackPack",0,0,0,random(0,2),random(0,2),random(3,6),random(0,360),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0) //Modify spawned items list as needed.  This is only a basic list of stuff spawned by the OmoiCaco upon it's death.
		HEAD AAAAA 0 A_SpawnItem("MedikitSpawner",1,16,0)
		HEAD A 0 A_SpawnItem("FSoulSphere",1,16,0)
		HEAD A 0 A_SpawnItem("MaxArmor",1,16,0)
	WeaponDrop:
		HEAD A 0 A_Jump(252,6)
		HEAD A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("OCWeaponDrop",4,"End")
		HEAD A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("OCWeapon1Check",1,4)
		HEAD A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("AEoDBFG9000Item",0,0,0,random(0,2),random(0,2),random(2,4),random(0,360),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		HEAD A 0 A_GiveInventory("OCWeapon1Check",1)
		HEAD A 0 A_GiveInventory("OCWeaponDrop",1)
		HEAD A 0 A_Jump(252,6)
		HEAD A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("OCWeaponDrop",4,"End")
		HEAD A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("OCWeapon2Check",1,4)
		HEAD A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("AEoDHEGrenadeLauncherItem",0,0,0,random(0,2),random(0,2),random(2,4),random(0,360),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		HEAD A 0 A_GiveInventory("OCWeapon2Check",1)
		HEAD A 0 A_GiveInventory("OCWeaponDrop",1)
		HEAD A 0 A_Jump(252,6)
		HEAD A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("OCWeaponDrop",4,"End")
		HEAD A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("OCWeapon3Check",1,4)
		HEAD A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("AEoDIncineratorItem",0,0,0,random(0,2),random(0,2),random(2,4),random(0,360),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		HEAD A 0 A_GiveInventory("OCWeapon3Check",1)
		HEAD A 0 A_GiveInventory("OCWeaponDrop",1)
		HEAD A 0 A_Jump(252,6)
		HEAD A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("OCWeaponDrop",4,"End")
		HEAD A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("OCWeapon4Check",1,4)
		HEAD A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("AEoDVulcanCannonItem",0,0,0,random(0,2),random(0,2),random(2,4),random(0,360),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		HEAD A 0 A_GiveInventory("OCWeapon4Check",1)
		HEAD A 0 A_GiveInventory("OCWeaponDrop",1)
		HEAD A 0 A_Jump(252,6)
		HEAD A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("OCWeaponDrop",4,"End")
		HEAD A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("OCWeapon5Check",1,4)
		HEAD A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("AEoDPlasmaRifleItem",0,0,0,random(0,2),random(0,2),random(2,4),random(0,360),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		HEAD A 0 A_GiveInventory("OCWeapon5Check",1)
		HEAD A 0 A_GiveInventory("OCWeaponDrop",1)
		HEAD A 0 A_Jump(252,6)

//===========================================================================
//
//	  Ever wondered how the founder of AEoD looks like? This is it.
//	  Except I dont fly nor have amazing powers... yet.
//
//===========================================================================
//		"The one you fear is protecting me"
//		"The one you pray to made me strong"
//		"The other one made me wise"
//===========================================================================
 
//No type
ACTOR FDeathBringerThanatos 7999
{
	var int user_counter[5];
	var int user_safeguard;
	var int user_inferno;
	var int user_bladecounter;
	var int user_damage;
	//[0] = Current number of steel counters
	//[1] = Refresh to max (7)
	//[2] = Take 1
	//[3] = Take 4
	//[4] = Take all
	Health 666666666
	Speed 9
	Radius 20
	Scale 0.6
	Height 56
	PainChance "Normal", 0
	PainChance "Massacre", 256
	PainChance "DBTKiller", 256
	+DONTTHRUST
	REACTIONTIME 1
	Monster	+DONTCORPSE 
	RipLevelMin 666
	+NOTELESTOMP
	+BOSSDEATH
	+BOSS
	+NOICEDEATH
	+FULLVOLACTIVE
	+FULLVOLDEATH
	+FORCERADIUSDMG
	//+NOTIMEFREEZE
	+DONTMORPH
	+NOFEAR
	+NODAMAGE
	+ALLOWPAIN
	BloodColor "Black"
	SeeSound "mon/dbt2/sight"
	DropItem Mana 255 600
	DropItem DarkMana 255 100
	DropItem AEoDHellHeavenHandItem
	DropItem RedMana 255 200
	
	//NOTICE! With the +NODAMAGE flag, he CANNOT be harmed!
	//This is simply done to allow infighting to happen!
	//He will remove +NODAMAGE and give himself an invulnerability failsafe
	//so he still gets damage through the normal DBTVulnerableThing way.
	//Thank you for taking the time to read this. -M.C.
	DamageFactor "Normal", 0.0 
	DamageFactor "Massacre", 0.000034
	
	Obituary "%o is now another slave to the Death Bringer."
	MinMissileChance 254

	States
	{
	Spawn:
		DBT2 B 0 NoDelay A_GiveInventory("IDied",1)
		//DBT2 B 0 A_SetUserVar(user_hp,health)
		DBT2 B 0 A_GiveInventory("Unrideable",1)
		DBT2 B 0 A_GiveInventory("DeathBringerToken",1)
		DBT2 B 0 A_SetUserArray("user_counter",0,0)
		DBT2 B 0 A_SetUserArray("user_counter",1,7)
		DBT2 B 0 A_SetUserArray("user_counter",2,1)
		DBT2 B 0 A_SetUserArray("user_counter",3,4)
		DBT2 B 0 A_SetUserArray("user_counter",4,0)
		DBT2 B 0 A_RemoveChildren(1) //ACS_Terminate(854,0)
	Idle:
		DBT2 B 0 A_JumpIfInventory("IDied",1,2)
		DBT2 B 0 A_GiveInventory("IDied",1)
		DBT2 B 0 A_UnSetFloat
		DBT2 B 0 A_Gravity
	Idle2:
		DBT2 B 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		DBT2 BBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBB 9 A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 A 0 A_SetFloat
		//TNT1 A 0 ACS_Execute(854,0,0,0,0)
		DBT2 A 0 A_NoGravity
		DBT2 A 0 ThrustThingZ(0,8,0,1)
		DBT2 AAAAAA 2 A_SpawnItem("DBTShadow",-1)
		DBT2 A 1 A_Stop
		DBT2 A 0 A_TakeInventory("IDied",1000)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DBTVoices",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
	Chasing:
		//"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar(user_damage,user_hp-health)
		//TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_safeguard!=1,4)
		//TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE",1)
		//TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("PowerDBTSafeGuard",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_safeguard",0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnSetReflective
		//TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SteelCounter",1,"RenderTrans")
		DBT2 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_counter[0]>=1,"RenderTrans")
		DBT2 A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1.0,0)
		DBT2 A 0 A_ResetHealth
	ChasingLoop:
		DBT2 A 2 A_Chase
		DBT2 A 0 A_SpawnItem("DBTShadow",0)
		Loop
	RenderTrans:
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.6,0)
		Goto "ChasingLoop"
	//Melee:	  //not used right now
	CircleStart:
		//TNT1 A 0 A_SpeedBalls
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("mon/dbt2/circleofdark",5,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("AltarBackFull",-5)								//PitChains attack - Death's Hand
		TNT1 A 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PillarSpawner",32,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PillarSpawnerLF",32,0,180)
		TNT1 A 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PillarSpawner",32,0,90)
		TNT1 A 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PillarSpawner",32,0,-90)
		TNT1 A 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PillarSpawnerLF",32,0,135)
		TNT1 A 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PillarSpawnerLF",32,0,-135)
		TNT1 A 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PillarSpawner",32,0,-45)
		TNT1 A 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PillarSpawner",32,0,45)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("Nakrul/Idlesight")
		DBT2 IJK 7
	CircleLoop:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("CircleCounter",10,"CircleEnd")
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("DBTMIM",0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("DBTMIM",0,0,45)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("DBTMIM",0,0,90)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("DBTMIM",0,0,135)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("DBTMIM",0,0,180)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("DBTMIM",0,0,-45)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("DBTMIM",0,0,-90)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("DBTMIM",0,0,-135)
		DBT2 K 5 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("DBTMIM",0,0,22)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("DBTMIM",0,0,67)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("DBTMIM",0,0,112)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("DBTMIM",0,0,157)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("DBTMIM",0,0,-22)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("DBTMIM",0,0,-67)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("DBTMIM",0,0,-112)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("DBTMIM",0,0,-157)
		DBT2 K 5 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("CircleCounter",1)
		Loop
	CircleEnd:
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("CircleCounter",12)
		DBT2 KJI 5
		Goto "Chasing"
 
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,"ChasingLoop") //was 190
		//TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("PowerDBTSafeGuard",1)
		//TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE",0)
		//TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_safeguard",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_inferno==1,"Missile2")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,"AttHeaven","AttAnger","AttSteel","AttKill","DefInferno","AttSlaughter","AttEvil","AttDeath")
	Missile2:
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_inferno",0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,"AttHeaven","AttAnger","AttSteel","AttKill","AttSlaughter","AttEvil","AttDeath")
	AttSteel:
		DBT2 A 0 A_PlaySound("mon/dbt2/steel",5,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
		DBT2 A 0 A_FaceTarget												   //Steel Attack - steel balls
		DBT2 A 7 bright A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 A 6 Bright A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_counter[0]>=1,"ASteelStl")//Inventory("SteelCounter",1,"ASteelStl")
		DBT2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DBTVulnerableThing",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThing")
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThingSteel")
		Goto "SteelEnd"
	ASteelStl:  
		DBT2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DBTVulnerableThingSteel",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		
		DBT2 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_counter",0,(user_counter[0]-user_counter[2]))
		Goto "SteelEnd"
	SteelEnd:
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThing")
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThingSteel")
		DBT2 AF 8 Bright
		DBT2 G 0 A_SetUserArray("user_counter",0,user_counter[1])							  //protected for 4 attacks
		DBT2 G 5 Bright
		DBT2 H 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("BallsofSteel",35,0,45)				 //couldnt help to do it :P
		DBT2 H 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("BallsofSteel",35,0,-45)
		DBT2 H 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("BallsofSteel",35,0,135)
		DBT2 H 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("BallsofSteel",35,0,-135)
		DBT2 HHHHHHHH 5 A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 G 0 A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 GF 8 Bright
		DBT2 AAA 7
		Goto "Chasing"
 
	AttKill:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("mon/dbt2/kill",5,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
		DBT2 A 0 A_FaceTarget												   //Kill attack - arch-vile type attack
		DBT2 C 7 A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 DE 6 A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 EE 6 Bright A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 E 0 A_JumpIf(user_counter[0]>=1,"AKillStl")
		DBT2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DBTVulnerableThing",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThing")
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThingSteel")
		TNT1 A 0 A_VileStart
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("KillDBTPartSpawnr",20,7,38,0,0,0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_VileTarget("KillMissile")
		Goto "KillCount"
	AKillStl:
		DBT2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DBTVulnerableThingSteel",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThing")
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThingSteel")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_counter",0,(user_counter[0]-user_counter[2]))
		TNT1 A 0 A_VileStart
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("KillDBTPartSpawnr",20,7,38,0,0,0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_VileTarget("KillMissile")
		Goto "KillCount"
	KillCount:
		DBT2 E 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AttackCounter",18,"KillCntEnd")
		DBT2 E 5 A_faceTarget
		DBT2 E 0 A_SpawnItemEx("KillDBTPartSpawnr",20,7,38,0,0,0,0,0)
		DBT2 E 0 A_VileTarget("KillMissile")
		DBT2 E 0 A_GiveInventory("AttackCounter",1)
		Loop
	KillCntEnd:
		DBT2 E 0 A_TakeInventory("AttackCounter",100)
		DBT2 E 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("PlayerToken",1,"KillPlayer")		//if player, goes to player check
		DBT2 E 4 Bright A_VileTarget("KillerMissileMonsters")				   //else, will deal a ton of damage
		Goto "KillEnd"
	KillPlayer:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfTargetInLOS("KillInSight",120)						 //if player still on sight, damages
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("AngerMissilePlayer",38,7,0)				   //otherwise, generic attack
		Goto "KillEnd"
	KillInSight:
		DBT2 E 4 Bright A_VileTarget("KillerMissilePlayer")					 //player damager
	KillEnd:
		DBT2 EEEEEEEEDC 8  
		Goto "Chasing"
 
	AttHeaven:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("mon/dbt2/heaven",5,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
		DBT2 A 0 A_FaceTarget												   //Heaven attack - surrounded by chains
		DBT2 A 0 A_CustomMissile("DBTCrucifix1",0,0,0)
		DBT2 A 7 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("HeavenChainMain1",0,0,30,10,0,0,45,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("HeavenChainMain2",0,0,30,10,0,0,-45,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("HeavenChainMain1",0,0,30,10,0,0,-135,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("HeavenChainMain2",0,0,30,10,0,0,135,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		DBT2 A 6 Bright A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_counter[0]>=1,"AHeavenStl")
		DBT2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DBTVulnerableThing",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThing")
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThingSteel")
		Goto "HeavenEnd"
	AHeavenStl:  
		
		DBT2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DBTVulnerableThingSteel",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThing")
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThingSteel")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_counter",0,(user_counter[0]-user_counter[3]))
		Goto "HeavenEnd"
	HeavenEnd:
		DBT2 I 8 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("HeavenProjSpawner",0,0,38,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		DBT2 J 8 Bright
		DBT2 K 5 Bright
		DBT2 KKKKKKKKKKK 5 Bright
		DBT2 KKKKKKKKKKK 5 Bright
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 JI 8 Bright
		DBT2 AAAAAA 7
		Goto "Chasing"
 
	AttSlaughter:
		DBT2 AA 8 A_FaceTarget												  //Slaughter attack - axes
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_counter[0]>=1,"AttSlaughterStl")
		DBT2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DBTVulnerableThing",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThing")
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThingSteel")
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("SteelCounter",1)
		Goto AttSlaughterEnd
	AttSlaughterStl:
		DBT2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DBTVulnerableThingSteel",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThing")
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThingSteel")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_counter",0,(user_counter[0]-user_counter[2]))
		Goto AttSlaughterEnd		   
	AttSlaughterEnd:
		DBT2 FG 8 bright
		DBT2 H 8 bright A_PlaySound("mon/dbt2/slaughter",5,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
		DBT2 H 0 A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 H 0 A_CustomMissile("SlaughterAxe",35,0,0)
		DBT2 H 0 A_CustomMissile("SlaughterAxe",35,0,120)
		DBT2 H 8 bright A_CustomMissile("SlaughterAxe",35,0,240)
		DBT2 H 0 A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 H 0 A_CustomMissile("SlaughterAxe",35,0,40)
		DBT2 H 0 A_CustomMissile("SlaughterAxe",35,0,160)
		DBT2 H 8 bright A_CustomMissile("SlaughterAxe",35,0,280)
		DBT2 H 0 A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 H 0 A_CustomMissile("SlaughterAxe",35,0,80)
		DBT2 H 0 A_CustomMissile("SlaughterAxe",35,0,200)
		DBT2 H 8 bright A_CustomMissile("SlaughterAxe",35,0,320)

		DBT2 H 0 A_JumpIf(user_bladecounter>=5,2) //A_JumpIfInventory("BladeCounter",5,2)
		DBT2 H 0 A_SetUserVar("user_bladecounter",user_bladecounter+1)//A_GiveInventory("BladeCounter",1)
		Goto AttSlaughterEnd+3
		DBT2 G 8 bright A_SetUserVar("user_bladecounter",0)//A_TakeInventory("BladeCounter",9999)
		DBT2 F 8 bright
		Goto "Chasing"
 
	AttAnger:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("mon/dbt2/anger",5,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
		DBT2 A 0 A_FaceTarget												   //Anger attack - homing fireball
		DBT2 C 7 A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 DE 6 A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 EE 6 Bright A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_counter[0]>=1,"AAngerStl")				//if protected
		DBT2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DBTVulnerableThing",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThing")
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThingSteel")
		Goto "AngerEnd"
	AAngerStl:
		DBT2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DBTVulnerableThingSteel",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThing")
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThingSteel")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_counter",0,(user_counter[0]-user_counter[2]))
		Goto "AngerEnd"
	AngerEnd:
		TNT1 a 0 A_SpawnItemEx("AngerParticleSpawner",20,7,38,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		DBT2 E 25 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("AngerSpawner",20,7,38,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 E 25 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("AngerSpawner",20,7,38,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 E 3 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("AngerSpawnerShort",20,7,38,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("PlayerToken",1,"AngerPlayer")
	AngerMonster:
		DBT2 E 4 Bright A_CustomMissile("AngerMissile",38,7,0)
		DBT2 EEEEEEEEDC 8
		Goto "Chasing"
	AngerPlayer:
		DBT2 E 4 Bright A_CustomMissile("AngerMissilePlayer",38,7,0)
		DBT2 EEEEEEEEDC 8
		Goto "Chasing"
 
	/*Soulsofdamned:  
		DBT2 A 0 A_FaceTarget												   //No longer used
		DBT2 A 0 ACS_Execute(855,0,6,0,0)  
		DBT2 AA 7 A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 FF 6 A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 G 6 Bright A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 F 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("OrbitGhostSpawner", 32, 0, 45)
		DBT2 F 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("OrbitGhostSpawner", 32, 0, -45)
		DBT2 F 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("OrbitGhostSpawner", 32, 0, -135)
		DBT2 H 7 Bright A_CustomMissile("OrbitGhostSpawner", 32, 0, 135)
		DBT2 HHHGGFF 6
		Goto "Chasing"*/
		 
	DefInferno:
		DBT2 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_inferno",1)
		DBT2 A 0 A_PlaySound("mon/dbt2/inferno",5,1,0,ATTN_NONE)									  //Inferno - defense
		DBT2 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_counter",0,user_counter[4])
		DBT2 A 8 A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 A 0 A_CustomMissile("DBTPentagram1",0,0,0)
		//DBT2 I 8 bright A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 I 0 bright A_SetReflective
		DBT2 I 0 bright A_CustomMissile("InfernoParticleSpawner",35,0,0)
		DBT2 I 0 bright A_CustomMissile("InfernoParticleSpawner2",35,0,0)
		DBT2 I 0 bright A_TakeInventory("DBTDamageCounter",random(100,500),0)
		DBT2 IIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIII 8 A_Explode(10,256,XF_NOTMISSILE,0,128)
		DBT2 AAAAAAA 5 A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 A 0 A_UnSetReflective
		Goto "Chasing"
	   
		AttEvil:
		DBT2 A 0 A_PlaySound("mon/dbt2/evil",5,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
		DBT2 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_counter[0]>=1,"AttEvilStl")
		DBT2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DBTVulnerableThing",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThing")
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThingSteel")
		Goto "AttEvilEnd"
		AttEvilStl:
		DBT2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DBTVulnerableThingSteel",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThing")
		//"####" "#" 0 A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableThingSteel")
		DBT2 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_counter",0,(user_counter[0]-user_counter[2]))
		Goto "AttEvilEnd"
		AttEvilEnd:
		DBT2 C 7 bright
		DBT2 DE 7 bright
		DBT2 E 0 bright A_CustomMissile("DBTEvilSkullShooter",38,7,90,2) //A_SpawnItemEx("DBTEvilSkull",20,-20,28,0,-25,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		DBT2 E 6 bright A_CustomMissile("DBTEvilSkullShooter",38,7,-90,2) //A_SpawnItemEx("DBTEvilSkull",20,20,28,0,25,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		DBT2 EEEEEE 6 bright
		DBT2 DC 7
		Goto "Chasing"
		
	AttDeath:								//THIS IS IT!!! -M.C.
		//Note for DBT: To play sounds at full volume regardless of distance, simply
		//put ATTN_NONE in the attenuation spot. This prevents fading via distance at all
		//and will always play until it ends or is interrupted.
		DBT2 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_counter",0,user_counter[4])
		DBT2 A 0 A_PlaySound("mon/dbt2/death",CHAN_VOICE,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
		DBT2 A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1.0,0)
		DBT2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DBTBlackFade",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
	Fader1:
		DBT2 A 2 A_FadeTo(0,0.025,0)
		DBT2 A 0 A_JumpIf(alpha<=0,1)
		Loop
		DBT2 I 0 A_PlaySound("mon/dbt2/wrathofgod",CHAN_AUTO,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
		DBT2 I 0 A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 IJ 10 A_FaceTarget
		DBT2 K 0 A_FadeTo(1,1,0)
		DBT2 K 0 bright A_SpawnItemEx("DBTWhiteFlash",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		DBT2 K 0 bright A_SpawnItemEx("DBTVulnerableDouble",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		"####" "#" 54 //A_DamageChildren(user_damage,"None",DMSS_NOFACTOR,"DBTVulnerableDouble")
		DBT2 K 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DBTAnkh1",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)//A_CustomMissile("DBTAnkh1",0,0,0)
		DBT2 K 0 A_PlaySound("brain/pain",CHAN_VOICE,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
		DBT2 KKKKKK 35 bright A_SpawnItemEx("DBTSGPortalMissile",10,0,35,20,0,0,random(0,359),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION) //A_CustomMissile("DBTDeathStorm",35,0,random(-10,10))
		DBT2 K 35
		DBT2 JI 8
		Goto "Chasing"
	Pain.DBTKiller:
		"####" "#" 1 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_Die
	Death:	
		"####" "#" 0 A_UnsetSolid
		DBT2 I 0 A_GiveInventory("IDied",1)
		DBT2 I 0 A_PlaySound("mon/dbt2/meetyoulater1",7,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
		DBT2 I 0 A_Fall
		DBT2 I 0 A_SetTranslucent(1.0,0)
		DBT2 I 12 Light("DBTDarkness") bright A_SpawnItemEx("BringerDeathI1",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		DBT2 J 12 Light("DBTDarknessTotal") bright A_SpawnItemEx("BringerDeathJ1",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		DBT2 K 30 Light("DBTDarknessTotal") bright A_SpawnItemEx("BringerDeathK1",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
	D1:
		DBT2 K 1 Light("DBTDarkness") bright A_FadeTo(0,0.02,FTF_CLAMP)
		DBT2 K 0 A_JumpIf(alpha <= 0.0,1)
		Loop
		TNT1 A 1 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,"None","AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	Pain.Massacre:
	Death.Massacre:
		DBT2 B 0 A_GiveInventory("IDied",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("mon/dbt2/deathoncheat",7,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
		DBT2 FGH 6
		DBT2 F 0 A_CustomMissile("CyberSpawner",2,0,0)
		DBTF H 1 A_FadeOut(0.05)
		Wait
	}
}

	Radius 38		//radius and height adjusted for a cyberdemon class monster

ACTOR FallenCherub 7521		// spider mastermind
{
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 
	Health 2000
	Radius 64
	Height 64
	Mass 90000000
	Speed 8
	PainChance 64
	Monster	+DONTCORPSE RipLevelMin 1 
	+BOSS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+MISSILEEVENMORE
	+NOICEDEATH
	+DONTMORPH
	+NOFEAR
	Scale 0.50
	Obituary "%o was no match for a Cherub class Angelique armor."
	SeeSound "CherubSight1"
	//DropItem CherubFlight	//this is better than A_SpawnItem for the jump :D
	//No it's not.
	DamageFactor "Wormwood", 0.2
	PainChance "Drain", 40
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	DamageFactor "ChaosExpl1", 0
	DamageFactor "ChaosExpl2", 0
//Holy
	DamageFactor "Unholy", 2.0
	DamageFactor "UnholyDisint", 2.0
	DamageFactor "AEMagic", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Holy", 0.5
	DamageFactor "Fire", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Electric", 0.75
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Plasma", 0.75
	DamageFactor "PlasmaDisint", 0.75
	States
	{
	Pain.Drain:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto Pain
	Spawn:
		ANGL A 4 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		ANGL JJKKLLMM 4 A_Chase	
		Loop
	Missile:
		ANGL B 0 A_Jump(128, "AkadiyamaMissiles")
	//Pulse Cannon
		ANGL I 10 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("diablo2/paladincast/fanaticism","SoundSlot5")
		ANGL I 26 A_PlaySound("CherubCharging")
		ANGL F 0 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile ("CherubFastShot", 60, 16, 0)
		ANGL F 4 BRIGHT A_PlaySound("CherubPulseCannon")
		ANGL G 4 A_CPosRefire
		Goto Missile+4
	AkadiyamaMissiles:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("diablo2/paladincast/defiance")
		ANGL N 10 A_FaceTarget
		ANGL N 4 A_CustomMissile("AkadMissile", 64, -20, 90)
		ANGL N 4 A_CustomMissile("AkadMissile", 64, 20, -90)
		ANGL N 4 A_CustomMissile("AkadMissile", 60, -20, 90)
		ANGL N 4 A_CustomMissile("AkadMissile", 60, 20, -90)
		ANGL N 4 A_CustomMissile("AkadMissile", 56, -20, 90)
		ANGL N 4 A_CustomMissile("AkadMissile", 56, 20, -90)
		ANGL N 4 A_CustomMissile("AkadMissile", 52, -20, 90)
		ANGL N 4 A_CustomMissile("AkadMissile", 52, 20, -90)
		Goto See
	Pain:
		ANGL B 0 A_Jump(96, 3)
		ANGL B 0 A_PlaySound("CherubPain")
		ANGL B 16 A_Pain
		Goto See
		ANGL O 0 A_PlaySound("CherubDefend")
		ANGL B 16 A_Pain
		Goto See
		ANGL O 4 A_SetInvulnerable
		ANGL P 4 A_FaceTarget
		ANGL Q 4 A_FaceTarget
		ANGL I 0 A_SetReflective
		ANGL I 90 A_CustomMissile("HaloFX", 32, 0, 0)
		ANGL I 0 A_UnSetReflectiveInvulnerable
		Goto See
	Death:	
		"####" "#" 0 A_UnsetSolid
		ANGL W 5 A_SpawnItem("CherubBodyDummy",0)
		ANGL X 70
		ANGL Y 70 A_PlaySound("CherubSight2")
		ANGL "Z[]" 5
		ANGL A 70
		ANGL B 0 A_Fall
		ANGL B 0 A_SpawnItemEx("CherubFlight",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_CLEARCALLERSPECIAL|SXF_CLEARCALLERTID,0,tid)
		Stop
	Death.Telefrag:
	Death.Massacre:
	XDeath.Telefrag:
	XDeath.Massacre:
	Death.Extreme.Telefrag:
	Death.Extreme.Massacre:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Fall
		TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("CherubFlight",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_CLEARCALLERSPECIAL|SXF_CLEARCALLERTID,0,tid)
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillChildren("None",KILS_FOILINVUL)
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,"None","AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	}
}

	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 
	Health 3000
	Radius 64
	Height 64
	Mass 99999991
	Speed 8
	PainChance 64
	Monster	+DONTCORPSE RipLevelMin 1 
	+FLOAT
	+NOGRAVITY
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+BOSS
	+MISSILEEVENMORE
	+LOOKALLAROUND
	+NOICEDEATH
	+DONTMORPH
	+NOFEAR
//	+CEILINGHUGGER
//	+SPAWNCEILING
	Scale 0.50

	DeathSound "CherubDeath"

	PainChance "Chaos", 255

	DamageFactor "ChaosExpl2", 0

	DamageFactor "Holy", 0.5
	DamageFactor "Fire", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Electric", 0.75
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Plasma", 0.75
	DamageFactor "PlasmaDisint", 0.75
	States
	{
	Pain.Drain:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)

		ANGL A 1 A_Look
		Loop

		ANGL B 1 A_NoGravity
		ANGL H 1 A_UnSetInvulnerable
		ANGL BBCC 3 A_FastChase

		ANGL DD 3 A_FastChase
		ANGL EE 2 A_FastChase
		Goto See+2

		ANGL B 0 A_Jump(80,"BombletRun")
	//PulseCannon
		ANGL I 10 A_FaceTarget

		ANGL I 35 A_PlaySound("CherubCharging")
		ANGL F 0 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile ("CherubFastShot", 60, 16, 0)
		ANGL F 4 BRIGHT A_PlaySound("CherubPulseCannon")
		ANGL G 4 A_CPosRefire
		Goto Missile+5
	AkadiyamaMissiles:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("diablo2/paladincast/defiance")
	ANG2 A 10 A_FaceTarget
	ANG2 A 4 A_CustomMissile("AkadMissile", 76, -20, 90)
	ANG2 A 4 A_CustomMissile("AkadMissile", 76, 20, -90)
	ANG2 A 4 A_CustomMissile("AkadMissile", 68, -20, 90)
	ANG2 A 4 A_CustomMissile("AkadMissile", 68, 20, -90)
	ANG2 A 4 A_CustomMissile("AkadMissile", 60, -20, 90)
	ANG2 A 4 A_CustomMissile("AkadMissile", 60, 20, -90)
	ANG2 A 4 A_CustomMissile("AkadMissile", 52, -20, 90)
	ANG2 A 4 A_CustomMissile("AkadMissile", 52, 20, -90)
		Goto See
	BombletRun:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("diablo2/necromancercast/taint","SoundSlot5")
		ANGL H 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("CherubAttack")
		ANGL H 10 A_FaceTarget
		ANGL H 1 A_SetInvulnerable
		ANGL H 1 A_SkullAttack
		ANGL H 0 A_Jump(64, 2)
		ANGL H 0 A_CustomMissile("Bomblet2", 76, -20, 90)
		ANGL H 0 A_Jump(64, 2)
		ANGL H 0 A_CustomMissile("Bomblet2", 76, 20, -90)
		ANGL H 0 A_Jump(64, 2)
		ANGL H 0 A_CustomMissile("Bomblet2", 60, -20, 90)
		ANGL H 0 A_Jump(64, 2)
		ANGL H 0 A_CustomMissile("Bomblet2", 60, 20, -90)
		ANGL H 0 A_Jump(64, 2)
		ANGL H 0 A_CustomMissile("Bomblet2", 44, -20, 90)
		ANGL H 0 A_Jump(64, 2)
		ANGL H 0 A_CustomMissile("Bomblet2", 44, 20, -90)
		ANGL H 0 A_Jump(64, 2)
		ANGL H 0 A_CustomMissile("Bomblet1", 44, -20, 80)
		ANGL H 0 A_Jump(64, 2)
		ANGL H 0 A_CustomMissile("Bomblet1", 44, 20, -80)
		ANGL H 0 A_Jump(64, 2)
		ANGL H 0 A_CustomMissile("Bomblet1", 28, -20, 80)
		ANGL H 0 A_Jump(64, 2)
		ANGL H 0 A_CustomMissile("Bomblet1", 28, 20, -80)
		ANGL H 0 A_Jump(64, 2)
		ANGL H 0 A_CustomMissile("Bomblet1", 12, -20, 80)
		ANGL H 0 A_Jump(64, 2)
		ANGL H 0 A_CustomMissile("Bomblet1", 12, 20, -80)
		ANGL H 0 A_PlaySound("CherubCluster")
	//40
	//25, 60
		ANGL H 1 A_CustomMissile("Exhaust", 40, 0, 0)
		ANGL H 0 A_CustomMissile("Exhaust", 60, 25, 0)
		ANGL H 0 A_CustomMissile("Exhaust", 60, -25, 0)
		ANGL H 1 A_CustomMissile("Exhaust", 40, 0, 0)
		ANGL H 0 A_CustomMissile("Exhaust", 60, 25, 0)
		ANGL H 0 A_CustomMissile("Exhaust", 60, -25, 0)
		Goto BombletRun+4
	Pain:
		ANGL B 0 A_Jump(100, 4)
		ANGL B 1 A_Gravity
		ANGL B 0 A_PlaySound("CherubPain")
		ANGL B 16 A_Pain
		Goto See
		ANGL O 4 A_SetInvulnerable
		ANGL P 4 A_FaceTarget
		ANGL Q 4 A_FaceTarget
		ANGL I 0 A_SetReflective
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("diablo2/paladincast/redemption")
		ANGL I 5 A_CustomMissile("HaloFX", 32, 0, 0)
		ANGL IIIIIIIIIIIIIIIII 5 A_CustomMissile("HaloShot",32,0,0)	//she must do something while defending.
		ANGL I 0 A_UnSetReflectiveInvulnerable
		Goto See
	Death:	
		"####" "#" 0 A_UnsetSolid
		ANGL R 5 A_Scream
		ANGL S 5
		ANGL T 5 A_CheckFloor("Crash")
		ANGL T 0 A_JumpIf(velz == 0,"Crash")
		Goto Death+2
	Crash:
		ANGL U 5 A_Fall
		ANGL V 0 A_QueueCorpse
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		ANGL V -1 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,"None","AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	}
}

		TNT1 A 0 A_SeekerMissile(1,1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(64,64,0)
		FX67 Y 1 A_SpawnItemEx("SLGFXtraSpawner",0,0,0,0,0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SeekerMissile(1,1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(64,64,0)
		Loop
	Death:
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	}

ACTOR ElementalCherub				   //Mancubus
{
	DropItem "AEoDRocketLauncherItem" 64
	DropItem "ExploAmmo"
	DropItem "ExploAmmo" 128
	DropItem "HealthHeart" 210
	DropItem "PowerslaveSpawner" 28
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 8
	Health 650 //Will not have a shield.
	Radius 30
	Height 56
	Mass 90000000
	Speed 8
	PainChance 128
	Monster	+DONTCORPSE RipLevelMin 1
	+BOSS //Will be needed (maybe?) for the MAP07 specials... If not, we can forget this flag.
	+BOSSDEATH
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+MISSILEEVENMORE
	+NOICEDEATH
	+DONTMORPH
	+NOFEAR
	Translation "209:255=%[0,0,0]:[0,1,0]", "160:171=%[0,0,0]:[0,1,0]", "48:79=%[0,0,0]:[0,1,0]"//, "172:175=%[0,0,0]:[0,1,0]"
	Scale 0.5
	Obituary "%o played Round Robin with the Elemental Cherub and lost."
	SeeSound "CherubSight1"
	DeathSound "CherubDeath"
	DamageFactor "Wormwood", 0.8
	PainChance "Charm", 96
	PainChance "Terror", 96
	PainChance "Drain", 64
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 128
	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 128
	//Armor
	DamageFactor "Electric", 1.5
	DamageFactor "Plasma", 0.75
	DamageFactor "PlasmaDisint", 0.75
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.5
	States
	{
	Pain.Charm:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)
		Goto See
	Pain.Terror:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)
		Goto See
	Pain.Drain:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto Pain
	Spawn:
		ANGL A 4 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		ANGL JJKKLLMM 4 A_Chase
		Loop
	Missile:
		ANGL I 0 A_JumpIfCloser(256,2) //If out of range from her target, lets have her skip the glyph.
		ANGL I 0 A_Jump(256,"IceBalls","MiniRockets","PoisonGlyphToss")
		ANGL I 0 A_Jump(256,"IceBalls","MiniRockets")
	IceBalls:
		ANGL I 10 A_FaceTarget
		ANGL I 20 A_PlaySound("CherubCharging")
		ANGL F 0 A_FaceTarget
		ANGL F 0 bright A_CustomMissile("CherubIceball", 50, 16, 0)
		ANGL F 8 bright A_PlaySound("CherubPulseCannon")
		ANGL G 8 A_CPosRefire
		Goto "IceBalls"+2
	MiniRockets:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("diablo2/paladincast/defiance")
		ANGL N 10 A_FaceTarget
		ANGL N 4 A_CustomMissile("CherubMissile", 50, -15, 30)
		ANGL N 4 A_CustomMissile("CherubMissile", 50, 15, -30)
		ANGL N 4 A_CustomMissile("CherubMissile", 50, -15, 30)
		ANGL N 4 A_CustomMissile("CherubMissile", 50, 15, -30)
		ANGL N 4 A_CustomMissile("CherubMissile", 50, -15, 30)
		ANGL N 4 A_CustomMissile("CherubMissile", 50, 15, -30)
		ANGL N 4 A_CustomMissile("CherubMissile", 50, -15, 30)
		ANGL N 4 A_CustomMissile("CherubMissile", 50, 15, -30)
		Goto See
	PoisonGlyphToss:
		ANGL LLLL 5 A_FaceTarget
		ANGL L 0 A_FaceTarget
		ANGL I 6 A_CustomMissile("CherubPoisonGlyph",64,10,0)
		Goto See
	Pain:
		ANGL B 0 A_Jump(96, 3)
		ANGL B 0 A_PlaySound("CherubPain")
		ANGL B 16 A_Pain
		Goto See
		ANGL O 0 A_PlaySound("CherubDefend")
		ANGL B 16 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:	
		"####" "#" 0 A_UnsetSolid
		ANGL R 0 A_Scream
		ANGL R 0 A_Fall
		ANGL RSTU 5
		ANGL V 0 A_QueueCorpse
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		ANGL V -1 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,"None","AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	Raise:
		ANGL VUTSR 7
		Goto See
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		"####" "#" 0 Thing_SetTranslation(0,50)
		"####" "#" 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,"None","AEoDSpawner")
		"####" "#" 1 A_FadeOut(0.015)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_Stop	
		"####" "#" 0 A_Fall
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateShadowMedium",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateSparksMedium",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "##" 2 A_FadeOut(0.03)
		Goto Disintegrate+6
	}
}

Actor PostalDude 		//cyberdemon
{
	DropItem "ShellBigAmmo" 160
	DropItem "ShellBigAmmo" 160
	DropItem "BulletBigAmmo" 160
	DropItem "BulletBigAmmo" 160
	DropItem "CellBigAmmo" 160
	DropItem "CellBigAmmo" 160
	DropItem "ExploBigAmmo" 160
	DropItem "ExploBigAmmo" 160
	DropItem "HealthHeart" 210
	DropItem "PowerslaveSpawner" 28
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 8
	DropItem "AEoDHERocketLauncherItem" 128
	DropItem "AEoDGoldenColtsItem" 128
	Monster	+DONTCORPSE RipLevelMin 1
	Health 7000
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Speed 14
	Painchance 30
	Mass 1500
	+BOSS
	+MISSILEMORE
	+MISSILEEVENMORE
	+FLOORCLIP
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+DONTMORPH
	+NOFEAR
	+FULLVOLDEATH
	MinMissileChance 1
	SeeSound "PostalDude/sight"
	PainSound "PostalDude/pain"
	DeathSound "PostalDude/Death"
	ActiveSound "PostalDude/idle"
	Scale 0.105
	DamageFactor "PostalDude", 0.05
	PainChance "PostalDude", 10
	MeleeRange 70
	PainChance "Charm", 0
	PainChance "Terror", 0
	PainChance "Defile", 0
	PainChance "Drain", 40
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	DamageFactor "ChaosExpl1", 0
	DamageFactor "ChaosExpl2", 0
//Armor
	DamageFactor "Electric", 1.5
	DamageFactor "Plasma", 0.75
	DamageFactor "PlasmaDisint", 0.75
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.5
	States
	{
	Pain.Chaos:
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl1",0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl2",0,0,0)
		Goto See
	Pain.ChaosExpl1:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ClearTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",1)
		Goto Spawn
	Pain.ChaosExpl2:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",0)		Goto See
	Pain.Drain:			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)	Goto Pain	
	
	Spawn:
		DUDE A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("PostalToken",8)
		DUDE BCDE 4 A_FastChase
		Loop
	Melee:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(80,"Missile")
		DUDE AAA 5 A_FaceTarget
		DUDE A 0 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(50,300),"postal2/weapons/shovel_hitbody","postal2/weapons/shovel_fire1")
		DUDE AA 4
		Goto See
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(512,"CloseAttack")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,"Machinegun","Shotgun","Pistol","RocketLauncher","RocketLauncherSeek")
	RocketLauncherSeek:
		DUDE A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		DUDE A 5 A_FaceTarget
		DUDE A 5 A_PlaySound("postal2/weapons/launcher_fueling",6)
		DUDE AAAAAAAA 10 A_FaceTarget
		DUDE A 5 A_PlaySound("postal2/weapons/launcher_seeker",6,1,0,0.3)
		DUDE AAAA 10 A_FaceTarget
		DUDE A 4 A_CustomMissile("PostalDudeRocketSeeker",32,0,0)
		DUDE A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,"See")
		TNT1 A 0 A_CposRefire
		Loop
	RocketLauncher:
		DUDE A 5 A_FaceTarget
		DUDE A 5 A_PlaySound("postal2/weapons/launcher_fueling",6)
		DUDE AAAA 10 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_StopSound(6)
		DUDE A 4 A_CustomMissile("PostalDudeRocket",32,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,"See")
		TNT1 A 0 A_CposRefire
		Loop
	Pistol:	//this one is special. The 1st and then every 8 (if successful) shots (explained why below) it will say
			//one of the "and one for..." lines. After it says all 7 lines available, it wont say them
			//again while in the same attack stream. If it reaches the "see" state, it will reset the
			//checks and whenever the pistol attack starts again, then it will start saying them again.
		DUDE BCD 5 A_Chase("","",CHF_FASTCHASE)		//calling the walking frames 1,2,3 & 4, here we start 1-2-3
		DUDE D 0 A_FaceTarget(0,0)
		DUDE A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("MonMuzzleFlash",7,5,35,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		DUDE A 0 A_PlaySound("postal2/weapons/pistol_fire",CHAN_WEAPON,0.5)
		"----" A 0 A_CustomMissile("BulletTracerFX",20,0,0,CMF_OFFSETPITCH,0)
		DUDE A 0 A_CustomBulletAttack(0,0,1,8,"PostalDudePuffCheck")	//notice how this is the only one that is special, only if it hits a target will activate
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("PostalToken",1,"MockChecker")
	PistolCont:
		DUDE EBC 5 A_Chase("","",CHF_FASTCHASE)		// 4-1-2
		DUDE C 1 A_FaceTarget(0,0)
		DUDE A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("MonMuzzleFlash",7,5,35,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		DUDE A 0 A_PlaySound("postal2/weapons/pistol_fire",CHAN_WEAPON,0.5)
		"----" A 0 A_CustomMissile("BulletTracerFX",20,0,random(-3,3),CMF_OFFSETPITCH,random(-3,3))
		DUDE A 0 A_CustomBulletAttack(3,3,1,8,"BulletDamagePuff")
		TNT1 A 0 A_CposRefire
		DUDE DEB 5 A_Chase("","",CHF_FASTCHASE)		// 3-4-1
		DUDE B 1 A_FaceTarget(0,0)
		DUDE A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("MonMuzzleFlash",7,5,35,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		DUDE A 0 A_PlaySound("postal2/weapons/pistol_fire",CHAN_WEAPON,0.5)
		"----" A 0 A_CustomMissile("BulletTracerFX",20,0,random(-3,3),CMF_OFFSETPITCH,random(-3,3))
		DUDE A 0 A_CustomBulletAttack(3,3,1,8,"PostalDudePuff")		//forces pain
		DUDE CDE 5 A_Chase("","",CHF_FASTCHASE)		// 2-3-4	so when it loops, it starts again from "1"
		DUDE E 1 A_FaceTarget(0,0)
		DUDE A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("MonMuzzleFlash",7,5,35,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		DUDE A 0 A_PlaySound("postal2/weapons/pistol_fire",CHAN_WEAPON,0.5)
		"----" A 0 A_CustomMissile("BulletTracerFX",20,0,random(-3,3),CMF_OFFSETPITCH,random(-3,3))
		DUDE A 0 A_CustomBulletAttack(3,3,1,8,"BulletDamagePuff")		//and it doesnt
		TNT1 A 0 A_CposRefire
	PistolCont2:
		//it repeats the whole thing here, because of the 4 stages shown above, and because then, every 8 will
		//check to say one of the "and one for..." phrases. Every 4 was too repeatedly, hence why i doubled that
		DUDE BCD 5 A_Chase("","",CHF_FASTCHASE)
		DUDE D 1 A_FaceTarget(0,0)
		DUDE A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("MonMuzzleFlash",7,5,35,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		DUDE A 0 A_PlaySound("postal2/weapons/pistol_fire",CHAN_WEAPON,0.5)
		"----" A 0 A_CustomMissile("BulletTracerFX",20,0,random(-3,3),CMF_OFFSETPITCH,random(-3,3))
		DUDE A 0 A_CustomBulletAttack(3,3,1,8,"PostalDudePuff")
		DUDE EBC 5 A_Chase("","",CHF_FASTCHASE)
		DUDE C 1 A_FaceTarget(0,0)
		DUDE A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("MonMuzzleFlash",7,5,35,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		DUDE A 0 A_PlaySound("postal2/weapons/pistol_fire",CHAN_WEAPON,0.5)
		"----" A 0 A_CustomMissile("BulletTracerFX",20,0,random(-3,3),CMF_OFFSETPITCH,random(-3,3))
		DUDE A 0 A_CustomBulletAttack(3,3,1,8,"BulletDamagePuff")
		TNT1 A 0 A_CposRefire
		DUDE DEB 5 A_Chase("","",CHF_FASTCHASE)
		DUDE B 1 A_FaceTarget(0,0)
		DUDE A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("MonMuzzleFlash",7,5,35,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		DUDE A 0 A_PlaySound("postal2/weapons/pistol_fire",CHAN_WEAPON,0.5)
		"----" A 0 A_CustomMissile("BulletTracerFX",20,0,random(-3,3),CMF_OFFSETPITCH,random(-3,3))
		DUDE A 0 A_CustomBulletAttack(3,3,1,8,"PostalDudePuff")
		DUDE CDE 5 A_Chase("","",CHF_FASTCHASE)
		DUDE E 1 A_FaceTarget(0,0)
		DUDE A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("MonMuzzleFlash",7,5,35,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		DUDE A 0 A_PlaySound("postal2/weapons/pistol_fire",CHAN_WEAPON,0.5)
		"----" A 0 A_CustomMissile("BulletTracerFX",20,0,random(-3,3),CMF_OFFSETPITCH,random(-3,3))
		DUDE A 0 A_CustomBulletAttack(3,3,1,8,"BulletDamagePuff")
		TNT1 A 0 A_CposRefire
		Goto Pistol
	MockChecker:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("PostalToken",8,"PistolCont2")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("PostalToken",7,"Mock7")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("PostalToken",6,"Mock6")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("PostalToken",5,"Mock5")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("PostalToken",4,"Mock4")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("PostalToken",3,"Mock3")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("PostalToken",2,"Mock2")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("PostalToken",1,"Mock1")
	Mock1:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("pd/x07",CHAN_VOICE,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
		Goto PistolCont
	Mock2:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("pd/x06",CHAN_VOICE,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
		Goto PistolCont
	Mock3:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("pd/x05",CHAN_VOICE,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
		Goto PistolCont
	Mock4:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("pd/x04",CHAN_VOICE,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
		Goto PistolCont
	Mock5:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("pd/x03",CHAN_VOICE,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
		Goto PistolCont
	Mock6:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("pd/x02",CHAN_VOICE,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
		Goto PistolCont
	Mock7:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("pd/x01",CHAN_VOICE,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
		Goto PistolCont
	Machinegun:
		DUDE A 4 A_FaceTarget(0,0)
		DUDE A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("MonMuzzleFlash",7,5,35,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(220,2)
		DUDE A 0 A_PlaySound("PostalDude/CatAttack",5,0.5)
		DUDE A 0 A_PlaySound("postal2/weapons/Machinegun_fire",CHAN_WEAPON,0.5)
		"----" A 0 A_CustomMissile("BulletTracerFX",20,0,random(-4,4),CMF_OFFSETPITCH,random(-4,4))
		DUDE A 2 A_CustomBulletAttack(4,4,1,5,"BulletDamagePuff")
		DUDE A 2 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(3,"See")
		TNT1 A 0 A_CPosRefire
		Goto Machinegun+1
	Shotgun:
		DUDE A 4 A_FaceTarget(0,0)
		DUDE A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("MonMuzzleFlash",7,0,35,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		DUDE A 0 A_PlaySound("PostalDude/CatAttack",5,0.5)
		DUDE A 0 A_PlaySound("postal2/weapons/shotgun_fire",CHAN_WEAPON,0.5)
		"----" AAAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("BulletTracerFX",20,0,random(-7,7),CMF_OFFSETPITCH,random(-6,6))
		DUDE A 5 A_CustomBulletAttack(7,6,8,6,"BulletDamagePuff")
		DUDE AA 5 A_FaceTarget 
		DUDE A 0 A_PlaySound("postal2/weapons/shotgun_ejectshell",5,0.5)
		DUDE BCDEB 5 A_Chase("","",CHF_FASTCHASE)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(40,"See")
		TNT1 A 0 A_CPosRefire
		Loop
	CloseAttack:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,"StinkyHead","Grenade")
	StinkyHead:
		DUDE A 0 A_PLaySound("postal2/weapons/cowhead_fire",CHAN_WEAPON,0.5)
		DUDE AAAAAAAA 4 A_FaceTarget
		DUDE A 0 A_PlaySound("reilsss/weapons/handGrenadethrow",CHAN_WEAPON,0.5)
		DUDE A 5 A_CustomMissile("PostalDudeStinkyHead",35,0,0)
		DUDE AAAAAAAA 10 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,"See")
		TNT1 A 0 A_CPosRefire
		Loop
	Grenade:
		DUDE A 0 A_PLaySound("postal2/weapons/grenade_pullpin",CHAN_WEAPON,0.5)
		DUDE AAAAA 4 A_FaceTarget
		DUDE A 0 A_PlaySound("reilsss/weapons/handGrenadethrow",CHAN_WEAPON,0.5)
		DUDE A 5 A_CustomMissile("ThrownGrenadeA",35,0,0)
		DUDE AAA 10 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,"See")
		TNT1 A 0 A_CPosRefire
		Loop
	Pain:
		DUDE A 4
		DUDE A 2 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:	
		"####" "#" 0 A_UnsetSolid
		DUDE G 5 A_Scream
		DUDE H 5 A_Fall
		DUDE I 5
		DUDE J 5 A_PlaySound("quake4/Misc/Body/Small")
		DUDE KL 5
		DUDE M 0 A_QueueCorpse
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		DUDE M -1 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,"None","AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	Death.Telefrag:
	XDeath.Telefrag:
	XDeath.Massacre:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
		TNT1 A 0 A_fall
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 AAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("QuakeGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,"None","AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	Ice:
		"####" "#" 5 A_GenericFreezeDeath
		"####" "#" 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,"None","AEoDSpawner")
		"####" "#" 1 A_FreezeDeathChunks
		Wait
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		"####" "#" 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,"None","AEoDSpawner")
		"####" "#" 0 Thing_SetTranslation(0,50)
		"####" "#" 1 A_FadeOut(0.015)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_Stop	
		"####" "#" 0 A_Fall
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateShadowMedium",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateSparksMedium",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "##" 2 A_FadeOut(0.03)
		Goto Disintegrate+7
	}
}

/*==============================================================================
//==============================================================================
								The Weeping Angel
INCOMING TRANSMISSION
Source: ANGRY ONE
Date:	UNKNOWN
Trace:	SUPERNATURAL ANOMALY DETECTED. ERROR -- CANNOT TRACK SOURCE.

						WARNING: INVALID RANGE DET-3zniAFCZ

Doctor, you made a grave mistake. You let them through to this universe. Now
what does it mean? Subjugation, corruption, and destruction of the highest
degree now burns in their essence. It ravages them, and they will burn at the 
end of time. This new unholy power they have consumed has made them vengeful.

Dangerously vengeful. The Dark One welcomes these supernatural creatures to help
remove the 'taint' that is humanity. Invested with the power of darkness, they
are more than capable of wiping out an entire city, in under thirty minutes.
They even kill their own kind, but that matters not. They will just keep pouring
forth to Earth, and make your world a permanent outpost of Hell.

			Clean up your mess, doctor. Don't make me do it for you.
//==============================================================================
//============================================================================*/

//archvile
Actor WeepingAngel
{
	var int user_turnangle;
	var int user_seen;
	var int user_warpangle;
	var int user_count;
	var int user_pseen;
	var int user_distance[2];
	//[0] = Used for warping
	//[1] = Used for distance checking
	Monster	+DONTCORPSE RipLevelMin 1
	Health 2000
	Speed 20
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Scale 0.31
	+BOSS
	+BOSSDEATH
	+NOPAIN
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+NOICEDEATH
	+NODAMAGE
	+NODAMAGETHRUST
	+FORCERADIUSDMG
	+FOILINVUL
	+DONTMORPH
	+ALLOWPAIN
	+DONTTHRUST
	+NOBLOOD
	DropItem "DemonMorphPowerup" 192
	DropItem "PowerupsSpawnerReal" 192
	DropItem "PowerupsSpawnerReal" 100
	DropItem "PowerupsSpawnerReal" 48
	DropItem "HalfWeaponPower"
	DropItem "RandomWeaponPower", 128
	//No type
	
	PainChance 0
	PainChance "Normal", 0
	PainChance "None", 0
	PainChance "Massacre", 256
	PainChance "Telefrag", 256
	SeeSound ""
	DeathSound "WeepingAngel/Death"
	MeleeRange 192
	DamageType "TempestLightning"
	PainType "Unholy"
	DeathType "Unholy"
	//Species "WeepingAngel"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		N080 A 0 NoDelay A_SpawnItemEx("WeepingAngelAura",0,0,32,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOPOINTERS|SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_SETTRACER|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N080 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WeepingAngelSightChecker",0,0,32,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		N080 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_turnangle",1)
		N080 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_distance",1,192)
		N080 A 0 A_PlaySound("WeepingAngel/Loop",7,1,1)
		N080 A 0 A_Warp(AAPTR_DEFAULT,0,0,0,0,WARPF_TOFLOOR)
		N080 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		N080 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE",0)
	Idle:
		N080 A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		N080 A 0 A_JumpIfTargetInLOS("Sight",360)
		N080 A 1 A_Chase
		Loop
	Sight:
		N080 A 0 A_PlaySound("WeepingAngel/See",CHAN_VOICE,1,0)
		N080 A 1 A_FaceTarget//(user_turnangle)
		//N080 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_turnangle >= 256,2)
		//N080 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_turnangle",user_turnangle*2)
		//N080 A 0 A_JumpIfTargetInLOS("Reset",10)
		//Loop
	//Check for the following:
	//1. Facing the actor within 90 degrees?
	//2. Do they run away first while keeping the angel in sight or do they turn first?
	Reset:
		N080 A 0 A_GiveInventory("WeepingAngelProtection",1)
		Goto RSCont
	Reset2:
		N080 C 0 A_GiveInventory("WeepingAngelProtection",1)
		Goto RSCont
	RSCont:
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserArray("user_distance",0,0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_turnangle",1)
	AirTime:
		"####" "#" 1 
		"####" "#" 0 A_CheckFloor("Waiting")
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(velz == 0,"Waiting")
		Loop
	Waiting: 
		"####" "#" 1 A_Chase("Melee","",CHF_DONTMOVE)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CheckClass("WeepingAngel",AAPTR_TARGET,0),"SpecialDeath")
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CheckClass("PlayerPawn",AAPTR_TARGET,1),1)
		Goto MonsterChase
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInLOS("Waiting",120,JLOSF_TARGETLOS) //#1 and 2 I hope...
	TargetNotLooking:
		"####" "#" 0 A_TakeInventory("WeepingAngelProtection",1000)
	TNL1:
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CheckClass("PlayerPawn",AAPTR_TARGET,1),"TNL2") //Slow it down for chasing the player.
		"####" "##" 0 A_Chase("Melee","")
	TNL2:
		"####" "#" 1 A_Chase("Melee","")
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInLOS("Waiting",120,JLOSF_TARGETLOS)
		//"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfCloser(192,"DistanceCheck")
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfCloser(1024,"TNL1")
		Goto PlayerCheck
		
	PlayerCheck:
		//Some wads insinuate on ClearInventory...
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CheckClass("PlayerPawn",AAPTR_TARGET,1),"PlayerCheckSuccess")
		Goto DistanceCheck
	PlayerCheckSuccess:
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_seen <= 0, "TNL1")

//DistanceCheck is used to warp to the target if they're too far away.
//Check to see if we can see it, then attempt to get behind them. If we find a
//spot, warp there and perform a sight check before anything else

	DistanceCheck:
		//"####" "#" 0 A_FaceTarget
		"####" "#" 0 A_CheckLOF("TargetNotLooking",CLOFF_SKIPOBSTACLES,1024,user_distance[1])
		Goto DC2
	DC2:
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserArray("user_distance",0,user_distance[0]+2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_Warp(AAPTR_TARGET,-user_distance[0],0,0,0,WARPF_INTERPOLATE|WARPF_COPYINTERPOLATION,"Respite")
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_distance[0] >= 250,"Reset")
		Loop
	Respite:
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CheckClass("PlayerPawn",AAPTR_TARGET,1),1)
		Goto MonsterSkip
		"####" "#" random(8,24)
		Goto RAPE
	MonsterChase:
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CheckClass("PlayerPawn",AAPTR_TARGET,1),"Waiting")
		"####" "#" 1 A_Chase("MonsterSkip","")
		Goto DistanceCheck
	RAPE:
	Melee:
		//Make sure not to attack from behind walls.
		"####" "#" 0 A_CheckLOF(1,CLOFF_SKIPFRIEND|CLOFF_SKIPNONHOSTILE|CLOFF_JUMPENEMY|CLOFF_SKIPOBJECT,user_distance[1])
		Goto Reset2
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CheckClass("PlayerPawn",AAPTR_TARGET,1),1)
		Goto MonsterSkip
		//D'ohshit it sees us! STAHP
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetLOS("Reset2",120)
	MonsterSkip:
		//"####" "#" 0 A_FaceTarget
		"####" "#" 0 A_Chase("","",CHF_DONTMOVE)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(IsPointerEqual(AAPTR_TARGET,AAPTR_NULL),"Reset2")
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfHealthLower(1,"Reset2",AAPTR_TARGET) //If it's dead, reset. Remember, LESS THAN for the function.
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInLOS(1,360)
		Goto Reset
		//"####" "#" 0 A_Warp(AAPTR_TARGET,-user_distance,0,0,0,WARPF_INTERPOLATE|WARPF_COPYINTERPOLATION|WARPF_USECALLERANGLE)
	MeleeMonster:
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("PlayerToken",1,"BACKSCRATCH",AAPTR_TARGET)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CheckClass("PlayerPawn",AAPTR_TARGET,1),"BACKSCRATCH")
		N080 C 0 A_Warp(AAPTR_TARGET,-user_distance[0],0,0,0,WARPF_INTERPOLATE|WARPF_COPYINTERPOLATION)
		N080 C 0 A_Explode(2,user_distance[1],XF_NOTMISSILE,1,user_distance[1])
		N080 C 1 A_DamageTarget(1000,"Unholy",DMSS_FOILINVUL)
		Goto MonsterSkip
	BACKSCRATCH:
		N080 C 0 A_Explode(2,user_distance[1],XF_NOTMISSILE,1,user_distance[1])
		N080 C 1 A_DamageTarget(random(1,5),"Unholy",DMSS_AFFECTARMOR)
		Goto RAPE
	SpecialDeath:
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOTARGETSWITCH",1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_FaceTarget
		"####" "#" 1 A_DamageTarget(3000,"Telefrag",DMSS_NOFACTOR|DMSS_KILL|DMSS_FOILINVUL)
	Pain.Massacre:
	Pain.Telefrag:	
		"####" "#" 1 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_UnsetInvulnerable
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE",0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_Die
	Death:	
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_Stop
		"####" "#" 0 A_Scream
		"####" "#" 0 A_StopSound(7)
		N080 C 140 A_SpawnItemEx("WADamnation",0,0,(z-floorz)+10,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_NOPOINTERS|SXF_SETMASTER) //Portal to Hell
		N080 A 0 A_Fall
		N080 AAAA 4 A_ChangeVelocity(0,0,-0.4)
	MoveDown:
		N080 A 5 
		N080 A 0 A_JumpIf(z <= (floorz-70),"End")
		Loop
	End:
		N080 A 70 A_GiveInventory("IDied",1)
	E2:
		N080 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_FadeOut(0.05,0)
		N080 A 0 A_Stop
		N080 A 70 A_GiveInventory("IDied",1)
		//N080 A 1 A_KillChildren("Normal",KILS_KILLMISSILES|KILS_NOMONSTERS)
		Stop
	}
}
