Actor WADCorner
{
	var int user_count;
	var int user_c2;
	var int user_x;
	var int user_scale[3];
	//[0] = Current
	//[1] = Maximum
	//[2] = Increment
	var int user_scale2;
	Projectile
	+NOINTERACTION
	+BRIGHT
	Translation "0:255=%[0.0,0.0,0.0]:[0.66,0.0,0.73]"
	RenderStyle Add
	Scale 0.0
	Alpha 0.75
//Let's see, want a constant growth and shrink in range of 50% of its normal scale,
//so 25% negative and 25% positive...
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		X099 A 0 NoDelay A_SetUserArray("user_scale",1,random(10,25))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserArray("user_scale",2,random(2,6))
		Loop1: //total distance between two points on a longer range is 286.
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WADLine",(14.3*user_x),0,3,0,0,0,18,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WADLine",(14.3*user_x),0,-3,0,0,0,-18,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_x",user_x+1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_x >= 19,1)
		Loop
		Playoff:
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_scale2 <= 359,2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scale2",0) //Let's not introduce runaway variables, just for safety.
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_scale[0] >= 900,"Waiting")
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserArray("user_scale",0,user_scale[0]+(user_scale[2]*2))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scale2",user_scale2+5)
		//Evaluate. Make sure it doesn't wind up negative, because if it does, it'll look weird. So in short,
		//force it to 0.
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(((sin(user_scale2)*0.10) + (sin((user_scale[0]*0.1)) * (user_scale[1]*0.01))*0.05) <= 0.0,2)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(((sin(user_scale2)*0.10) + (sin((user_scale[0]*0.1)) * (user_scale[1]*0.01))*0.05))
		Loop
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0)
		Loop
		Waiting:
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserArray("user_scale",0,900)
	W2:
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_scale2 <= 359,2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scale2",0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scale2",user_scale2+5)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_count >= (35*60),"Death")
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("IDied",2,"Death",AAPTR_MASTER)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_count",user_count+1)
		//Shouldnt be needed here, but sanity check is for sanity.
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(((sin(user_scale2)*0.10) + (sin((user_scale[0]*0.1)) * (user_scale[1]*0.01))*0.05) <= 0.0,2)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(((sin(user_scale2)*0.10) + (sin((user_scale[0]*0.1)) * (user_scale[1]*0.01))*0.05))
		Loop
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0)
		Loop
	Death:
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_scale[0] <= 0,2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserArray("user_scale",0,user_scale[0]-15)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf((user_scale[0] <= 0) && (ScaleX <= 0.0),"End")
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_scale2 <= 359,2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scale2",0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scale2",user_scale2+5)
		//Evaluate. Make sure it doesn't wind up negative, because if it does, it'll look weird. So in short,
		//force it to 0.
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(((sin(user_scale2)*0.10) + (sin((user_scale[0]*0.1)) * (user_scale[1]*0.01)*0.05)) <= 0.0,2)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(((sin(user_scale2)*0.10) + (sin((user_scale[0]*0.1)) * (user_scale[1]*0.01)*0.05)))
		Loop
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0)
		Loop
	End:
		TNT1 A 0
		Stop
	}
}

Actor WADLine
{
	var int user_count;
	var int user_s;
	Projectile
	+NOINTERACTION
	+BRIGHT //I dont feel like putting this on every single frame. No thanks.
	Scale 0.1
	RenderStyle Add
	Alpha 0.0
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		X099 A 0 NoDelay A_SetUserVar("user_s",random(0,359))
	Sizing:
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_count >= 30,2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_FadeIn(0.01)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_count",user_count+1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_s <= 359,2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_s",0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_s",user_s+5)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale((sin(user_s)*0.02)+0.05)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("IDied",2,"Death",AAPTR_MASTER)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_count >= (35*60), "Death")
		Loop
	Death:
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_count",user_count+1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_s <= 359,2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_s",0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_s",user_s+5)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale((sin(user_s)*0.02)+0.05)
		"####" "#" 0 A_FadeOut(0.01)
		Loop
	}
}

Actor WeepingAngelSightChecker
{
	Monster
	-COUNTKILL
	+NONSHOOTABLE
	-SHOOTABLE
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	+NOINTERACTION
	+LOOKALLAROUND
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfHealthLower(1,"End",AAPTR_MASTER) //Our health check...
		TNT1 A 17 A_LookEx(LOF_NOSOUNDCHECK,0,0,0,360,"See")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Warp(AAPTR_MASTER,0,0,32,0,WARPF_NOCHECKPOSITION,"Spawn") //...and our existence check.
		Goto End
	See:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("WASeenCheck",1,AAPTR_MASTER)
	End:
		TNT1 A 0
		Stop
	}
}

Actor WeepingAngelAura
{
	var int user_dist;
	var int user_offset[2];
	//[0] = Jump
	//[1] = Effect
	var int user_count[2];
	//[0] = Current
	//[1] = Max
	+NOINTERACTION
	+BRIGHT
	Scale 0.25
	Alpha 0.65
	RenderStyle Add
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		X122 ABCD 1 bright A_Warp(AAPTR_MASTER,0,0,28,0,WARPF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		X122 D 0 bright A_SetUserArray("user_offset",0,2)
		Goto Puffing
	A2:
		X122 EFGH 1 bright A_Warp(AAPTR_MASTER,0,0,28,0,WARPF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		X122 H 0 bright A_SetUserArray("user_offset",0,3)
		Goto Puffing
	A3:
		X122 IJKL 1 bright A_Warp(AAPTR_MASTER,0,0,28,0,WARPF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		X122 L 0 bright A_SetUserArray("user_offset",0,4)
		Goto Puffing
	A4:
		X122 MNOP 1 bright A_Warp(AAPTR_MASTER,0,0,28,0,WARPF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		X122 P 0 bright A_SetUserArray("user_offset",0,1)
		Goto Puffing
	Puffing:
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("IDied",1,"End",AAPTR_MASTER)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserArray("user_count",0,0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserArray("user_count",1,random(1,5))
	PuffLoop:
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserArray("user_offset",1,random(0,359))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_dist",random(-100,-150))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WeepingAngelSmoke",
			(cos(user_offset[1])*user_dist),0,(sin(user_offset[1])*user_dist),
			(cos(user_offset[1])*2),0,(sin(user_offset[1])*2),random(0,359),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserArray("user_count",0,user_count[0]+1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_count[0] >= user_count[1],"Continue")
	Continue:
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_offset[0] <= 1, "Spawn")
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_offset[0] == 2, "A2")
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_offset[0] == 3, "A3")
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_offset[0] >= 4, "A4")
		Goto Spawn
	End:
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_offset[0] <= 1, "E1")
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_offset[0] == 2, "E2")
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_offset[0] == 3, "E3")
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_offset[0] >= 4, "E4")
	E4:
		X122 EFGH 1 A_FadeOut(0.02)
	E3:
		X122 IJKL 1 A_FadeOut(0.02)
	E2:
		X122 MNOP 1 A_FadeOut(0.02)
	E1:
		X122 ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOP 1 A_FadeOut(0.02)
		Loop
	}
}

Actor WADSmokeStream
{
	var int user_count;
	var int user_cur[2];
	var int user_distance[3];
	//[0] = current
	//[1] = multiplier (taking it by 40, so 7.15)
	//[2] = max (143)
	+MISSILE
	+NOINTERACTION
	Renderstyle None
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		TNT1 A 0 NoDelay A_SetUserArray("user_distance",2,143000)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_distance",1,3575) //We must multiply it by .01. These cant handle floats.
		//TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_cur",1,user_distance[1])
		Looping:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_distance[0] >= user_distance[2],2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_distance",0,user_distance[0]+user_distance[1])
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("IDied",1,"LoopOut",AAPTR_MASTER)
		Loop2:
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WeepingAngelSmoke",(random(user_cur[0],user_cur[1])*0.001),0,frandom(0.0,10.0),0,0,frandom(2.0,8.0),SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_ABSOLUTEPOSITION,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,250,32760)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WeepingAngelSmoke",(random(user_cur[0],user_cur[1])*0.001),0,frandom(0.0,10.0),0,0,frandom(2.0,8.0),-18,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,250,32760)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_cur",0,user_cur[1])
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_cur",1,user_cur[1]+user_distance[1])
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_cur[1] >= user_distance[0],1)
		Loop
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_cur",0,0)
		TNT1 A 1 A_SetUserArray("user_cur",1,0)
		Goto Looping
		LoopOut:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_distance[0] <= user_distance[1],"End")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_distance",0,user_distance[0]-user_distance[1])
		Loop3:
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WeepingAngelSmoke",(random(user_cur[0],user_cur[1])*0.001),0,frandom(0.0,10.0),0,0,frandom(2.0,8.0),SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_ABSOLUTEPOSITION,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,250,32760)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WeepingAngelSmoke",(random(user_cur[0],user_cur[1])*0.001),0,frandom(0.0,10.0),0,0,frandom(2.0,8.0),-18,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,250,32760)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_cur",0,user_cur[1])
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_cur",1,user_cur[1]+user_distance[1])
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_cur[1] > user_distance[0],1)
		Loop
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_cur",0,0)
		TNT1 A 1 A_SetUserArray("user_cur",1,user_distance[1])
		Goto LoopOut
	End:
		TNT1 A 0
		Stop
	}
}


Actor WeepingAngelSmoke
{
	var int user_sx;
	var int user_sy;
	var int user_scale[3];
	var int user_alt;
	//[0] = Current
	//[1] = Maximum
	//[2] = Increment
	+MISSILE
	+NOINTERACTION
	RenderStyle Translucent
	Alpha 0.2
	Scale 0.0
	Translation "0:255=%[0,0,0]:[0.2,0,0.6]"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		TNT1 A 0 NoDelay A_JumpIf(tid == 0,"S2") //No division by zero.
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_alt",tid/tid)
		TNT1 A 0 A_FadeTo(0.0,0.6,0)
		Goto S3
	S2:
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_scale",1,random(10,20))
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_scale",2,random(6,12))
	S3:
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_sx",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_sy",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_sx",-1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,"R1")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_sy",-1)
		Goto R1
		Playoff:
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_alt > 0,"Playoff2")
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_scale[0] >= 900,2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserArray("user_scale",0,user_scale[0]+user_scale[2])
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetScale(sin(((user_scale[0]*0.1)) * (user_scale[1]*0.1))*user_sx,sin(((user_scale[0]*0.1)) * (user_scale[1]*0.1))*user_sy)
		"####" "#" 1
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("IDied",1,"FastFade",AAPTR_MASTER)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_scale[0] <= 400,"Playoff")
		"####" "#" 0 A_FadeOut(0.01)
		Loop
	FastFade:
		"####" "#" 0 A_FadeOut(0.1)
		Goto Playoff
		Playoff2:
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetScale(frandom(0.15,0.30)*user_sx,frandom(0.15,0.30)*user_sy)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetAngle(random(0,359))
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeVelocity(frandom(0.0,4.0),0,0,CVF_RELATIVE)
		"####" "##########" 1 A_FadeIn(0.04)
		"####" "##########" 1 A_ScaleVelocity(0.975)
	P2E:
		"####" "#" 0 A_ScaleVelocity(0.975)
		"####" "#" 1 A_FadeOut(0.05)
		Loop
	R1:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,"T","U","V","W")
	T:		X038 ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUV 0 A_JumpIf(random(1,22) == 1,"Playoff")	Goto Playoff
	U:		X039 ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUV 0 A_JumpIf(random(1,22) == 1,"Playoff")	Goto Playoff
	V:		X040 ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUV 0 A_JumpIf(random(1,22) == 1,"Playoff")	Goto Playoff
	W:		X041 ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUV 0 A_JumpIf(random(1,22) == 1,"Playoff")	Goto Playoff
	}
}
